Cisco UI Base

 

Typography updated

We use CiscoSans as primary
CiscoSans includes ExtraLight, ExtraLightOblique, Light, LightOblique, Regular, and Bold. The font stack in order is CiscoSans, Arial, Sans-Serif
Font formats supported include woff and woff2. (woff is needed to support IE 11)

typography Headings

By default the UI kit supports auto-scaling of header (h1-h6) font sizes. This means that at smaller breakpoints you do not have to add any special media queries to scale down header sizes as it is handled automatically.

Specify the CSS class modifier cui--fixed-headers at the top-level to change to using fixed header (h1-h6) font sizes.

Jan Tschichold

Albert Einstein

Mark Twain

Grid System new

We have adopted the Bootstrap 4 Grid system which has 5 grid tiers and is Flexbox-based
You can view more details on the grid here

grid Breakpoints

  Extra Small (<576px) Small (>=576px) Medium (>=768px) Large (>=992px) Extra Large (>=1200px)
Class prefix .col- .col-sm- .col-md- .col-lg- .col-xl-
View Source Copy 
<div class="responsive-table">
    <table class="table table--bordered table--compressed">
        <thead>
            <tr>
                <th>&nbsp;</th>
                <th>Extra Small (<576px)</th>
                <th>Small (>=576px)</th>
                <th>Medium (>=768px)</th>
                <th>Large (>=992px)</th>
                <th>Extra Large (>=1200px)</th>
            </tr>
        </thead>
        <tbody>
            <tr>
                <td>Class prefix</td>
                <td>.col-</td>
                <td>.col-sm-</td>
                <td>.col-md-</td>
                <td>.col-lg-</td>
                <td>.col-xl-</td>
            </tr>
        </tbody>
    </table>
</div>

input States

Use javascript to add/remove the class modifiers to/from the input tag in each form-group element.

Supported class modifiers include:
input--dirty Input field is dirty (has been touched)
input--valid Input field is valid (this is the default state)
input--invalid Input field is invalid
input--invalid-required Input field is invalid because it is required
This is a required field
Special characters not allowed
View Source Copy 
<div class="row">
    <div class="col-md-6">
        <form>
            <div class="form-group">
                <div class="form-group__text">
                    <input id="text1" type="text">
                    <label for="text1">Text</label>
                </div>
            </div>
            <div class="form-group">
                <div class="form-group__text">
                    <input id="text3" type="text" disabled>
                    <label for="text3">Text (disabled)</label>
                </div>
            </div>
            <div class="form-group">
                <div class="form-group__text">
                    <input id="text2" type="text" required>
                    <label for="text2">Text (required)</label>
                    <div class="required-block">
                        <span class="icon-asterisk"></span>
                    </div>
                </div>
            </div>
            <div class="form-group">
                <div class="form-group__text">
                    <input id="text4" type="text" class="input--dirty input--valid" value="Lorem Ipsum" required>
                    <label for="text4">Text (required, dirty, valid)</label>
                    <div class="required-block">
                        <span class="icon-asterisk" title="This is a required field"></span>
                    </div>
                </div>
            </div>
            <div class="form-group form-group--helper">
                <div class="form-group__text">
                    <input id="text5" type="text" class="input--dirty input--invalid-required" value="" required>
                    <label for="text5">Text (required, dirty, invalid-required)</label>
                    <div class="required-block">
                        <span class="icon-asterisk" title="This is a required field"></span>
                    </div>
                </div>
            <div class="help-block text-warning">
                <span class="icon-exclamation-triangle"></span>
                <span>This is a required field</span>
            </div>
            </div>
            <div class="form-group form-group--helper">
                <div class="form-group__text">
                    <input id="text6" type="text" class="input--dirty input--invalid" value="&#^$&(%$" required>
                    <label for="text6">Text (required, dirty, invalid)</label>
                    <div class="required-block">
                        <span class="icon-asterisk" title="This is a required field"></span>
                    </div>
                </div>
            <div class="help-block text-danger">
                <span class="icon-error"></span>
                <span>Special characters not allowed</span>
            </div>
            </div>
        </form>
    </div>
</div>

input Text Area

You will need to use javascript to dynamically grow/shrink the textarea. Something similar to the jQuery Elastic plugin or Angular Elastic directive
Add the attribute or class disabled to the input element to denote a disabled field.
Add the attribute or class readonly to the input element to denote a read-only field
View Source Copy 
<div class="row">
    <div class="col-md-6">
        <form>
            <div class="form-group">
                <div class="form-group__text">
                    <textarea id="textarea1" rows="1"></textarea>
                    <label for="textarea1">Textarea</label>
                </div>
            </div>
        </form>
    </div>
    <div class="col-md-6">
        <form>
            <div class="form-group">
                <div class="form-group__text">
                    <textarea id="textarea2" rows="1" readonly></textarea>
                    <label for="textarea2">Textarea (readonly)</label>
                </div>
            </div>
        </form>
    </div>
</div>

List

Lists are a fundamental collection pattern that can be used as a container for other components

Since: 1.0.0

list Spacing / Vertical

Spacing between elements in a list can be specified using the modifiers shown below. This is useful when you need to manage spacing (margins) between your components

Spacing (default)

Compressed

Regular

Loose

View Source Copy 
<div class="row">
    <div class="col-md-3">
        <p>Spacing (default)</p>

            <li><div class="panel panel--bordered"><img src="public/img/short-paragraph.png"></div></li>
            <li><div class="panel panel--bordered"><img src="public/img/short-paragraph.png"></div></li>
            <li><div class="panel panel--bordered"><img src="public/img/short-paragraph.png"></div></li>

            <li><div class="panel panel--bordered"><img src="public/img/short-paragraph.png"></div></li>

Row 3, Column 1 Row 3, Column 2 Row 3, Column 3

table Striping

By default all rows are striped for better visibility. Add the class table--nostripes to remove row striping

With Striping (default)

Header 1 Header 2 Header 3
Row 1, Column 1 Row 1, Column 2 Row 1, Column 3
Row 2, Column 1 Row 2, Column 2 Row 2, Column 3
Row 3, Column 1 Row 3, Column 2 Row 3, Column 3

No Striping

Header 1 Header 2 Header 3
Row 1, Column 1 Row 1, Column 2 Row 1, Column 3
Row 2, Column 1 Row 2, Column 2 Row 2, Column 3
Row 3, Column 1 Row 3, Column 2 Row 3, Column 3

table Fixed

Add the class table--fixed to change the table layout to fixed. A fixed table layout renders quicker than non-fixed but column widths are not determined by the data. By default tables are NOT fixed

table Padding

Compressed

Header 1 Header 2 Header 3

Row 2, Column 1 Row 2, Column 2 Row 2, Column 3
Row 3, Column 1 Row 3, Column 2 Row 3, Column 3

Regular (default)

Header 1 Header 2 Header 3
Row 1, Column 1 Row 1, Column 2 Row 1, Column 3
Row 2, Column 1 Row 2, Column 2 Row 2, Column 3
Row 3, Column 1 Row 3, Column 2 Row 3, Column 3

Loose

Header 1 Header 2 Header 3
Row 1, Column 1 Row 1, Column 2 Row 1, Column 3
Row 2, Column 1 Row 2, Column 2 Row 2, Column 3
Row 3, Column 1 Row 3, Column 2 Row 3, Column 3
